    <script src="/static/js/index.js"></script>
    <script src="/static/js/toast.js"></script>
    <script src="/static/js/user_preferences.js"></script>
    <script>
        // 更新最近玩过的游戏列表
        function updateRecentGamesList() {
            const recentGamesList = document.getElementById('recentGamesList');
            if (!recentGamesList) return;

            let playedGames = [];
            try {
                const stored = localStorage.getItem('playedGames');
                if (stored) {
                    playedGames = JSON.parse(stored);
                    
                    // 确保没有重复游戏（通过链接进行去重）
                    const uniqueGames = [];
                    const seenLinks = new Set();
                    
                    for (const game of playedGames) {
                        if (!seenLinks.has(game.link)) {
                            seenLinks.add(game.link);
                            uniqueGames.push(game);
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // 用去重后的列表替换原来的列表
                    playedGames = uniqueGames;
                    
                    // 更新本地存储中的去重列表
                    localStorage.setItem('playedGames', JSON.stringify(playedGames));
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('Error reading from localStorage:', e);
            }

            if (playedGames.length === 0) {
                recentGamesList.innerHTML = "<div class='no-games'>No recently played games</div>";
                return;
            }

            recentGamesList.innerHTML = playedGames
                .map(game => `
                    <a href="${game.link}" class="recent-game-item">
                        <img src="${game.img}" alt="${game.title}" class="recent-game-img">
                        <span class="recent-game-title">${game.title}</span>
                    </a>
                `)
                .join('');
        }

        // 清除游戏历史
        function clearPlayedGames() {
            if (confirm("Are you sure you want to clear your game history?")) {
                localStorage.removeItem('playedGames');
                updateRecentGamesList();
                // 触发自定义事件通知其他页面更新列表
                const event = new CustomEvent('playedGamesUpdated');
                window.dispatchEvent(event);
            }
        }

        // 监听存储更新事件
        window.addEventListener('playedGamesUpdated', updateRecentGamesList);
        
        // 监听存储变化
        window.addEventListener('storage', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'playedGames') {
                updateRecentGamesList();
            }
        });

        // 页面加载时初始化
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            updateRecentGamesList();
            
            // 语言选择器功能
            document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
                const languageSelector = document.getElementById('languageSelector');
                if (languageSelector && !languageSelector.contains(event.target)) {
                    languageSelector.classList.remove('active');
                }
            });
        });
        
        // 切换语言选择器菜单
        function toggleLanguageMenu(event) {
            if(event) {
                event.preventDefault();
                event.stopPropagation();
            }
            const languageSelector = document.getElementById('languageSelector');
            if(!languageSelector) return;
            
            // 切换活动状态
            languageSelector.classList.toggle('active');
            
            // 如果打开了菜单，添加事件监听器以处理外部点击关闭
            if(languageSelector.classList.contains('active')) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    document.addEventListener('click', closeLanguageMenuOnClickOutside);
                }, 10);
            } else {
                document.removeEventListener('click', closeLanguageMenuOnClickOutside);
            }
        }
        
        // 在菜单外部点击时关闭菜单
        function closeLanguageMenuOnClickOutside(event) {
            const languageSelector = document.getElementById('languageSelector');
            if(languageSelector && !languageSelector.contains(event.target)) {
                languageSelector.classList.remove('active');
                document.removeEventListener('click', closeLanguageMenuOnClickOutside);
            }
        }
    </script>
    
    <!-- 多语言文本存储区域(隐藏) -->
    <div id="languageStrings" style="display:none;">
        <div id="favAddedText">Game added to favorites</div>
        <div id="favRemovedText">Game removed from favorites</div>
        <div id="clickViewGameText">Click to view game</div>
    </div>
